<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tónkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>thinly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not thickly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li>delicately, finely (e.g. of produced workmanship)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкость</a> (8108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tónkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tónkostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thinness, fineness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкость</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильтрация.html>фильтра́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tónkostʹ filʹtrácii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">filtering capacity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>slenderness, slimness</li>
<li>delicacy, finesse</li>
<li>subtlety, finesse, fineness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкость</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tónkostʹ uma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">subtlety of mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкость</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tónkostʹ rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fine workmanship</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fine point, nicety, subtlety
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкостей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do tónkostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to a nicety</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдаваться.html>вдава́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкость.html>то́нкости</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdavátʹsja v <b>tónkosti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">subtilize, split hairs</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нна</a> (3404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tonne</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tónna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>metric ton, tonne (1000 kilograms)</li>
<li>large number, large amount, large weight</li>
<li>ton</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a thousand units

***тонуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>тону́ть</a> (6113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>тону́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tonútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потонуть.html>потону́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затонуть.html>затону́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утонуть.html>утону́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sink, to go down</li>
<li>to drown</li>
<li>to be lost
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>то́нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ненужный.html>нену́жных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подробность.html>подро́бностях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">myslʹ tónet v nenúžnyx podróbnostjax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the idea is lost in a mass of unnecessary details</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>тону́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tonútʹ v deláx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be up to one's eyes in work, to be snowed under with work</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тоня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоня.html>то́ня</a> (4631)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тонꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tonja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*topnь</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tорni̯а</i>, related to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">topítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоня.html>то́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tónja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоня.html>то́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоня.html>то́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоня.html>то́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fishery, fishing ground</li>
<li>haul of fish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>то́пить</a> (6561)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*topìti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">topítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истопить.html>истопи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натопить.html>натопи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stoke (an oven)</li>
<li>to heat</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*topìti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (same as Etymology 1).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">topítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растопить.html>растопи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to melt, to render (fat)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*topìti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">topítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потопить.html>потопи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затопить.html>затопи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утопить.html>утопи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sink</li>
<li>to drown (transitive)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to support (a club or political party)</li>
<li>to topple (a person involved in politics, a student during exam)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drive (as qualifier "against the rules" or "much quicker than usually")</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топиться.html>топи́ться</a> (16585)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">topítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топиться.html>топи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">topítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утопиться.html>утопи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drown oneself</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to melt</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be lit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a stove</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">topítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">topítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потопить.html>потопи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potopítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топка.html>то́пка</a> (14176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">topítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топка.html>то́пка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tópka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топка.html>то́пки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топка.html>то́пки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топка.html>то́пок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heating, stoking</li>
<li>fire chamber, furnace, firebox</li>
<li>melting (down)</li></ol>

***топкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топкий.html>то́пкий</a> (17998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топить.html>топи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">topítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sink, to drown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топкий.html>то́пкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tópkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)то́пче</b>, <i>abstract noun</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">то́пкость</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>oozy, mucky, boggy, marshy, miry, quaggy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">describing wet ground or muck into which one's feet may sink</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1918</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleksey_Nikolayevich_Tolstoy" class="extiw" title="w:Aleksey Nikolayevich Tolstoy"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Н. <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a></a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>День</a> Петра</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводнение.html>наводне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смывать.html>смыва́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:опустошать.html>опустоша́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожар.html>пожа́р</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лод</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:косить.html>коси́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́д</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снова.html>сно́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тянуться.html>тяну́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:топкий.html>то́пким</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лесной.html>лесны́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тропа.html>тро́пам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каменщик.html>ка́менщиков</a>, дровору́бов, бочкаре́й, кожемя́к.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Navodnénija smyváli rabótu, opustošál jejó požár; gólod i jázva kosíli naród, i snóva tjanúlisʹ po <b>tópkim</b> dorógam, po lesným trópam pártii kámenščikov, drovorúbov, bočkaréj, kožemják.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Floods would wash away the construction sites, fires would devastate them, hunger and disease would ravage the workers, and so more parties of stonemasons, lumberjacks, coopers, tanners would come creeping down <b>muck-covered</b> roads and forest footpaths.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1955</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Varlam_Shalamov" class="extiw" title="w:Varlam Shalamov"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a>. Т. Шаламов</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:татарский.html>Тата́рский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>мулла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>воздух</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>тону́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:топкий.html>то́пком</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мох.html>мхе</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:летний.html>ле́тний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухи́ми</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nogá tonúla v <b>tópkom</b> mxe, i rédko za létnij denʹ nógi býli suxími.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Feet sank in the <b>quaggy</b> moss, and few were the summer days when feet would be dry.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топкий.html>то́пкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tópkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)то́пче</b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> easily stoked, providing plenty of heat</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топливо.html>то́пливо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóplivo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топливный.html>то́пливный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóplivnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fuel, petrol</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топливо.html>то́пливо</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tóplivo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<ol><li>n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Метанол является удобным энергоносителем, который можно использовать в качестве моторного, котельного и газотурбинного топлива, как источник водорода для <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">топливных</span> элементов. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

***тополь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>то́поль</a> (5911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*topolь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>то́поль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tópolʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>то́поля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>тополя́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>то́поли</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>тополе́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тополь.html>то́полей</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Poetic.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>poplar (any of various deciduous trees of the genus Populus)</li>
<li>cottonwood</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тополёк</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">topoljók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***топор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топо́р</a> (1959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">топоръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toporŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poleaxe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*toporъ</i>. Further etymology is disputed.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">topór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топора́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топоры́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топоро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>axe, ax, hatchet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топо́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">plávatʹ kak topór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">swim like a stone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***топот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топот.html>то́пот</a> (7688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топот.html>то́пот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tópot</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топот.html>то́пота</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>footfall, tread, tramp, trample, stamp, stomp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торопливый.html>торопли́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:топот.html>то́пот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаго́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">toroplívyj <b>tópot</b> šagóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sound of hurried footsteps; patter of feet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:топот.html>то́пот</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kónskij <b>tópot</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">thud/clatter of horses' hoofs</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***топтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a> (7821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">тъпътъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭpŭtŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and thus related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топот.html>то́пот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tópot</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">footfall, tread, tample</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include Template:bog, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">deptat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">dерtаć</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toptátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to trample down</li>
<li>to tread dirt <i>(into)</i>, to leave dirty footmarks <i>(on)</i>, to track dirt <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ботинок.html>боти́нками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>toptátʹ</b> pol grjáznymi botínkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mark up the floor with one's dirty boots</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глина.html>гли́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>toptátʹ</b> glínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knead clay</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear <i>(shoes)</i> unsparingly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топчи́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зря.html>зря</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туфля.html>ту́фли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>topčí</b> zrja nóvyje túfli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't walk around in your new shoes without a reason</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to trample <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:достоинство.html>досто́инство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>toptátʹ</b> čʹjó-libo dostóinstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trample on someone's dignity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(of fowl)</i> to cover, to mount</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">trample down</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ута́птывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">utáptyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">trample</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раста́птывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rastáptyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:топтаться.html>топта́ться</a> (6365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toptátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтаться.html>топта́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toptátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shift one's feet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтаться.html>топта́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">toptátʹsja na méste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mark time, make no headway</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang about, to hang around, to loiter, to wait</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dawdle, to dillydally</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toptátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">shift one's feet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переминаться.html>перемина́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pereminátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
